    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer3618401570106456023">In <i>New York Times </i>and <i>USA TODAY </i>bestselling author Kresley Cole’s sizzling series, a fierce werewolf and a bewitching vampire become unlikely soul mates whose passion will test the boundaries of life and death.<br/><br/>After enduring years of torture from the vampire horde, Lachlain MacRieve, leader of the Lykae Clan, is enraged to find the predestined mate he’s waited millennia fo</span>
  <span id="freeText3618401570106456023" style="display:none">In <i>New York Times </i>and <i>USA TODAY </i>bestselling author Kresley Cole’s sizzling series, a fierce werewolf and a bewitching vampire become unlikely soul mates whose passion will test the boundaries of life and death.<br /><br />After enduring years of torture from the vampire horde, Lachlain MacRieve, leader of the Lykae Clan, is enraged to find the predestined mate he’s waited millennia for is a vampire. Or partly one. Emmaline Troy is a small, ethereal half Valkyrie/half vampire, who somehow begins to soothe the fury burning within him.<br /><br />Sheltered Emmaline finally sets out to uncover the truth about her deceased parents—until a powerful Lykae claims her as his mate and forces her back to his ancestral Scottish castle. There, her fear of the Lykae—and their notorious dark desires—ebbs as he begins a slow, wicked seduction to sate her own dark cravings.<br /><br />Yet when an ancient evil from her past resurfaces, will their desire deepen into a love that can bring a proud warrior to his knees and turn a gentle beauty into the fighter she was born to be?</span>
  <a data-text-id="3618401570106456023" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class='communityQuestion'>
<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/524444-i-just-came-across-this-series-as-audible">I just came across this series as Audible has the whole series on for $4.95 per book for a few days. I bought the first 2 but don&#39;t know if I should buy them all. Here&#39;s the questions: is it mainly romance? Do characters recur or is it new protagonist(s) each book? If it&#39;s pure romance and new characters I probably don&#39;t need more than 2.</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_524444'><a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/24210536-harley-andrade"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1481785696i/24210536._UX100_CR0,16,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/24210536-harley-andrade">Harley Andrade</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">It is mainly romance, every book is about a different matted pair. It is a new pair each time but there is overlapping characters as minor/medium char<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">It is mainly romance, every book is about a different matted pair. It is a new pair each time but there is overlapping characters as minor/medium characters. I still suggest reading them all because I love this series and haven't gotten tired of it like I did with christen feehan or Lyndsay sands.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer102764564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15434784113188352184">I DESPISE this kind of rape-glorifying bullshit! We have the innocent half vampire girl chased all over town by psycho madman who makes several starts to raping the terrified girl and has her crying and begging, then lo and behold just as he is about to 'do' her she suddenly feels desire for him and off we head to lovey dovey land despite him treating her like shit. This shit sickens me to the bloody stomach and I hate to see this kind of forced sex used as entertainment and wrapped up with pink</span>
  <span id="freeText15434784113188352184" style="display:none">I DESPISE this kind of rape-glorifying bullshit! We have the innocent half vampire girl chased all over town by psycho madman who makes several starts to raping the terrified girl and has her crying and begging, then lo and behold just as he is about to 'do' her she suddenly feels desire for him and off we head to lovey dovey land despite him treating her like shit. This shit sickens me to the bloody stomach and I hate to see this kind of forced sex used as entertainment and wrapped up with pink bows and paraded as romance and seduction. If men on the street behaved like this I somehow doubt that we'd see it as fluffy bunny romance-we'd be screaming blue murder! I know this is fiction and the excuse is his tortured past but it still isn't the slightest bit erotic or romantic to me,just plain sick.<br /><br />***Dec 2016 update...dear dear I was a bit irate when I wrote it but I feel strongly about rape being turned into love and romance. At the time I tended to vent rather than explain. However I am more measured in my reviews now and want to clarify a couple of things:<br /><br />-I am not having a go at anyone who reads and enjoys these books as it is fiction and everyone has the right to enjoy their reading. So if you enjoy this kind of book I'm not trying to say there is something wrong with you! This is just my personal opinion on the plot.<br /><br />-I don't mean this as an attack on the actual author, just the subject matter being used. I'm not trying to say there is something wrong with the author for writing this plot. <br /><br />So there we are. If you like the author and the plot, please continue to do so and just ignore my venting!***</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/260575073" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/260575073?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=shifters-or-weres">shifters-or-weres</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=highlanders">highlanders</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer260575073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6913422262938482387">***Re-read 10/7/15. Rating bump from 3 to 4 stars. Original review below. *** <br/><br/><i>...meanwhile, inside of the Fetish Cafe...</i><br/><br/><i>Waitress :</i> Miss? Are you ready to order?<br/><br/><i>Me :</i> (clearing throat) Um, I think so? Can you tell me first if there are any off-the-menu specials tonight?<br/><br/><i>Waitress :</i> Nothing extra tonight. Our supplier didn't deliver today, so we're running low on supplies. If you're looking for a fantasy involving props, chances are, it's not going to happen.<br/><br/><i>Me :</i> It's fine. That's not really my thing</span>
  <span id="freeText6913422262938482387" style="display:none">***Re-read 10/7/15. Rating bump from 3 to 4 stars. Original review below. *** <br /><br /><i>...meanwhile, inside of the Fetish Cafe...</i><br /><br /><i>Waitress :</i> Miss? Are you ready to order?<br /><br /><i>Me :</i> (clearing throat) Um, I think so? Can you tell me first if there are any off-the-menu specials tonight?<br /><br /><i>Waitress :</i> Nothing extra tonight. Our supplier didn't deliver today, so we're running low on supplies. If you're looking for a fantasy involving props, chances are, it's not going to happen.<br /><br /><i>Me :</i> It's fine. That's not really my thing. (pause) Uh...I think I'll take the kidnapping special. With an order of dominant male. Preferably tall, dark, handsome, and pushy...you know the drill. The alpha type.<br /><br /><i>Waitress :</i> Big spender, aren't we? Anything else? (says sarcastically) Would you like fries with your order?<br /><br /><i>Me :</i> Yes, please. Can I get some gravy with that on the side? Brown, not white.<br /><br /><i>Waitress :</i> (appearing a bit confused) Whatever. It's your fetish.<br /><br /><i>Me :</i> Oh no. The fries aren't part of it. I'm just hungry.<br /><br />.....<br /><br />Trigger warning : content borders on rapey (yes, it's a word, dammit)<br /><br />Eh, what can I say? <i>A Hunger</i> was a fun and fluffy read. There's no real substance here, but when comparing this to other pnr, it's on par with others that I've liked. Which is not bad, considering I've been on a serious adult pnr break lately after trying a few I didn't like. They're all starting to read the same and I've passed on most of the ones which haven't had more of an urban fantasy bent. Straight-up adult romance novels (in most every genre) have been pretty disappointing to me lately, so I've chosen not to go there. Until now. I saw a few friends talking about this one and figured I'd give it a shot. <br /><br />I find it funny that if this book were realistic fiction, I would rip it up one side and down the other for having such a horrible male lead. As in : NO ONE SHOULD READ THIS BOOK. The male lead is pushy, demanding, forceful, and about 20 other things which would have any female running for the hills in absolute horror. If some guy (or girl) pulled this act on me or anyone I know, I'd call the cops and have him (or her) locked up. <br /><br />But of course, I tend to cave a little for fantasy based books. What can I say? I have a thing for alpha men in pnr and historicals. Plus, this one had an ancient scottish brogue! Well, hellooooo highlander. Thank you for showing up in my kidnap story.<br /><br />At least, in this book, I get to give the double argument for his lack of decorum. <br /><br />1. It's pnr. These aren't guys raised in polite society. They're driven by instinct that overwhelms them. Bad excuse? Sure. But hey, it's the basis for most pnr shifter stories. The devil made them do it, or some other nonsense. We laugh at it, we find it far-fetched, we'd hate it if any man in real life treated us like this, but darnit...it's fun to read about in books.<br /><br />2. The dude is old. Like pre-dating historical bodice-ripping, non-con storylines, OLD. As in, "he came from the dirt" old. Historical fiction readers know that men from the past weren't as clued in to the equality of men and women. They always seem to need a woman to school them. And our heroine in this story did, in fact, school her man.<br /><br /><b>Who I'd recommend this book to :</b><br /><br />People who don't mind aggressive alphas in their pnr and can forgive some <i>serious</i> bad behavior if the hero shows some sign of remorse or willingness to change later.<br /><br /><b>Who I'd warn away from the book :</b><br /><br />Anyone who has a previous history of abuse, whether physical or sexual. The hero(?) did push the boundaries of sex and crossed some lines that he shouldn't have. The book danced that line of danger a little too close for comfort at times <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[going down on someone in their sleep because you want to make them feel good <i>is</i> still against a person's will (and therefore wrong), even if it's not violent or scarring (in this instance) sexual experience....or making them take a shower with you, etc. It's still not okay. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Anyone who rolls their eyes at old stereotypes of cavemen-type males. I'm warning you - you will hate this book. It's okay to steer clear. In fact, why are you even reading this review? You might want to go shower all of the gunk off now. Hurry! <br /><br />No, really. I don't blame anyone who would find this book distasteful. Only us fluff cravers are going to enjoy <i>A Hunger</i>. And enjoy, I did. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6913422262938482387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_35542624" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/35542624" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/35542624?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of paranormal romance, especially werewolves</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to  Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books) by: </span>
      2013 IAD group series reread
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=captive-kidnapped">captive-kidnapped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=2013-iad-series-reread">2013-iad-series-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scarred-hero">scarred-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=revenge">revenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scottish">scottish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer35542624" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4687925021176523853"><b>Third Reread Completed in September 2020.<br/><br/>I listened to this on Audio, and I think I finished in a few days. That's just how fantastic this book is. This book helped get me into paranormal romance, and I haven't looked back since. The narrator, Robert Petkoff's work is a thing of beauty. His Scottish accent is flawless. His Eastern European accents are excellent. I found his accent for Emmaline interesting, almost like an 19th Century, highly educated Southern accent. That makes sense, she is chr</b></span>
  <span id="freeText4687925021176523853" style="display:none"><b>Third Reread Completed in September 2020.<br /><br />I listened to this on Audio, and I think I finished in a few days. That's just how fantastic this book is. This book helped get me into paranormal romance, and I haven't looked back since. The narrator, Robert Petkoff's work is a thing of beauty. His Scottish accent is flawless. His Eastern European accents are excellent. I found his accent for Emmaline interesting, almost like an 19th Century, highly educated Southern accent. That makes sense, she is chronologically 70 (although appears to be in her early twenties). <br /><br />Although books are a lot edgier now than they used to be, this still feels edgy and new/exciting/distinctive to me, and this book is 14 years old. Super hot and steamy and wow. Obsessive hero, check. I had forgotten how borderline mean Lachlan was to Emmaline at first. I'm so glad Emmaline came into herself and learned to stand up for herself against an aggressive mate and overbearing and aggressive family members. I could definitely see myself in her (minus the aggressive mate). Kresley Cole really hit it out of the park with this series and this first full book in the series. It stands up just as well almost 20 years later. I will definitely be rereading the other books. I'm glad that I have fallen back into the Paranormal Romance Zone. It's helping me right now with escapism and helping to rekindle my book reading love. If you haven't read the Immortals After Dark series, what are you waiting for??? </b><br />*********<br /><br />2nd Reread Completed 8/1-8/9/13<br /><br />Looking back at how much I loved this book when I first read it, and how much I loved it on reread, I can say most definitely that this book is an all-time keeper. For me, this story is magic. I didn't have a lot of time to read it, but I actually didn't want to put it down when I couldn't read it. Finally, when I was able to dedicate some time to reading, I more or less read it straight through, except for when I was busy with my review books and Vacation Bible School. At the end of the night, I was excited to get into bed and curl up and revisit Lachlain and Emma's love story, reading late into the night.<br /><br /><b>Lachlain</b><br /><br />Lachlain remains one of my fall time favorite paranormal heroes (and probably of all time). Although I refuse to pick a favorite Immortals After Dark hero, Lachlain makes some steep competition for the following heroes. He starts out a bully, but I can understand why. He literally was insane after being tortured for 150 years. However, it is a testament to his force of will that he didn't do worse to Emmaline, not to mention the power of their bond. Even though he wasn't super nice initially, his charisma was undeniable. As time passes and he realizes who Emma is and how she means to him, above and beyond being his fated mate, he shows just how adoring and capable of caring for his mate he can be. By the time Emma starts to love him, you can understand why. Cole makes you want a Lykae mate of your very own. <br /><br /><b>Emmaline</b><br /><br />Sometimes the heroine doesn't click with me in a romance. But this is not one of those times. I loved Emma. I appreciated her journey of self-identity and coming into her own. She had that awkward feel of a woman on the cusp of maturity in her early twenties. Away from home for the first time, exploring who she is, and finding love. Considering the force of nature that Lachlain is, I think Emma held her own against him, and eventually, she had him eating out of her hand.<br /><br />I think Kresley Cole writes the best steamy romance out there. Blazingly hot, but not crossing the line into raunchy and distasteful (overshare) language that turns 'sexy' into 'gross' for this reader. Even on the reread, I was excited to see what happened next, and fanning myself with the incredible tension and fire between Emma and Lachlain. I wasn't a huge fan of vampire romance prior to reading this (this being one of the first I read at the time), but the scenes in which Lachlain feeds Emma show how powerful that is between a mated pair, and it's sexy, and not gross like I always thought it would be. I'm not saying I want to take blood or give my blood like in the book, but it's written well and beliveable in the context of the story. It's a very intimate thing, and you could see how it furthers the connection between them.<br /><br />On top of the fantastic romance, the world-building is complex and fascinating, and I love the camaraderie between the Valkyries and the other characters. You can see the Lore factions aligning before your eyes on the one way march to the Ascension. And though the developing romance is fascinating, it's also great to get glimpses into the past of the long-lived creatures of the Lore. <br /><br />There's a reason why Kresley Cole is in my top five authors of all time. She knows how to bring it. In the paranormal and historical romance genres, she kicks butt and takes names. You want to keep coming back for more of this wonderful world she has created. I'm glad I was able to revisit this fantastic book and I am jazzed to continue my 2013 reread of the Immortals After Dark series.<br /><br /><br /><b>Check out my <a href="http://pinterest.com/gatadelafuente/immortals-after-dark-series-by-kresley-cole/" rel="nofollow noopener">Immortals After Dark Pinboard</a> on Pinterest.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br />****Original Review Below*********<br />I bought this book because I had read "If You Dare," by this author and absolutely loved it. Well, lets just say, it made a steadfast fan of me. The Immortals After Dark is one of my all time favorite paranormal series, and part of the reason I'm so crazy about paranormals. Lachlain is kind of crazy, and who can blame him after being imprisioned horribly underground in a fiery pit, being drowned every day and consumed by fire for 150 years. One day he senses his mate, and he does something really painful and desperate to get free, to get to her. I was hooked. <br /><br />Lachlain is what I call a Sexy, Scottish, Werewolf. What a great combination. His one shortcoming is that he is kind of snobby towards Emmaline at first. He's dismayed that this true mate (Lykae only get one) is a Vampire. Although she's really a halfling, half-vampire, half-valkyrie. Emmaline is as timid as you can get. She's been protected and coddled by her valkyrie aunts her whole young life. She's about 70 years old, which is very young for a vampire and a valkyrie. Despite her penchant for very sexy, expensive lingerie, she's an innocent virgin. <br /><br />Imagine this crazed, beastly man tearing across a Paris courtyard, and dragging you off with him, and wanting to do things with you of a sexual nature? Very scary thought. This is how this book begins. Cole grabbed me as a reader and didn't let go. I wanted to find out how Lachlain would deal with the fact that his mate was not exactly what he wanted. Would he force her? Would she grow to love him and trust him? They go on a journey to get back to Lachlain's ancestral holdings in Scotland. He is the king of the Lycae and must go back to take his place as ruler of his people. Even though he isn't really happy with the mate that was chosen for him by fate, he's taking her with him. Lochlain has to get used to modern life. He finds he has expensive tastes, and charges up poor Emmaline's platinum card. He really makes the poor girl miserable. But she does manage to fall in love with him. She's not so sure about this Queen of the Lykae deal and having such a dominant mate, though. So it takes some serious wooing, Lykae-style, on Lachlain's part. And Lachlain discovers that having a vampire bride is a great thing, because being bitten by her is ecstasy. Plus, Emmaline is a sweet, loving woman who eases her way into his heart. <br /><br />This was a fabulous book. I was already werewolf-inclined after reading the MaryJanice Davidson story "Love's Prisoner", Bitten by Kelley Armstrong, and Night Play by Sherrilyn Kenyon, so it really got my attention. This is a spicy read with very hot love scenes, that don't overshadow the growing love between Lachlain and Emmaline. I enjoyed the whole dynamic of reluctant mates, and the crazy, alpha werewolf hero really appealed to me. I loved how Lachlain's feelings towards his bride changed so that he came to adore her and appreciate her. She became his life. I also loved how timid Emmaline comes into her own. She was drifting because she knew neither of her parents. She was afraid and disliked her vampire nature, and had to come to terms with who she is. She becomes quite the warrior queen. Ah, this is a classic for me. It comes highly recommended. <br /><br />Just a warning to readers. The first book in this series is the story in Playing Easy to Get, "The Warlord Wants Forever." I read this one first and I was scratching my head trying to figure out who Nikolai and Myst were. You can read this first, but you might be a little lost when they bring up Nikolai and Myst as a forgone conclusion.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4687925021176523853" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_161228895" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/161228895" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/161228895?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2011">2011</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer161228895" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1810306833783192650"><br/><b>2.5 Stars</b> simply for the inexplicable need the novel induced in me to keep on reading despite the many reasons not to. I actually find it quite surprising that I didn't abandon the book after the first few chapters featured numerous attempted rape scenes, a control freak of a man (or male, at least) whose violent tendencies are not only portrayed as acceptable, but highly desirable. But, though I was immediately horrified, the book also somehow managed to hold my attention and the writing style,</span>
  <span id="freeText1810306833783192650" style="display:none"><br /><b>2.5 Stars</b> simply for the inexplicable need the novel induced in me to keep on reading despite the many reasons not to. I actually find it quite surprising that I didn't abandon the book after the first few chapters featured numerous attempted rape scenes, a control freak of a man (or male, at least) whose violent tendencies are not only portrayed as acceptable, but highly desirable. But, though I was immediately horrified, the book also somehow managed to hold my attention and the writing style, a strange interest in the plot, and a morbid fascination in this destructive relationship forced me to read on.<br /><br />I'm not at all in favour of this kind of unhealthy relationship where the guy relentlessly pursues a woman, scares her into submission, and attempts to rape her so many times that she eventually decides he's kinda hot. I do not find this an appealing romance story. If it was a cautionary tale of abusive relationships... well, then sure! But <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a> seems to celebrate the controlling personality of Lachlain and I find it rather disturbing to see how highly rated this book is. Apparently, he's so "gorgeous" and "sexy" and "protective" and these traits all make up for the fact that he repeatedly sexually assaults Emma, refuses to let her return to her family, demands that she sleep in the same bed as him (to her obvious discomfort as her kind are known for preferring to sleep on the floor), and even picks out the clothes she wears. <i>He picks out the clothes she wears</i>. This is not a romance, it's the story of one person completely taking over the life of another, refusing to let them make any decisions for themselves and calling it love.<br /><br />Can someone actually let me know why so many rate this book highly? It's not much of an urban fantasy because there's just a random array of creatures that hate each other and no great mythological story going on... and it certainly doesn't work as a romance. Or do I not understand the idea of romance and love? Yeah, I'm 19, perhaps it's me who doesn't get it... but I thought it was about caring, compassion and <b>mutual respect</b>. I honestly want to understand why I read this book and saw abuse when <i>thousands</i> have read this and seen love and sexiness.<br /><br />And yes, there were some attempts to redeem Lachlain... he began to understand that he had treated Emma badly and felt very guilty that he had nearly strangled her to death... <i>aww, poor Lachlain...</i> *rolls eyes* Whatever happened later, I never supported their violent relationship; plus, even though Lachlain experienced some minor guilt for the attempted rapes/choking, it didn't affect him enough to let Emma make any decisions for herself... nope, she <b>must</b> stay with him and she <b>must</b> sleep with him, but this time she <b>must</b> like it too! Good god. It was painful to read.<br /><br />Why not 1 star? There were good bits amongst the annoying. I quite liked the scenes where they just talked in the car and he began to learn about the 21st century after being locked up for a couple hundred years; his reaction to the plastic card that has unlimited possibilities was funny, so was his repetitive opening and closing of the sun roof. But there was more of what I don't want to read than what I do want to. I can't and won't wrap my head around the idea of a guy finding his one true mate and treating her in such a cruel, violent and often openly humiliating way. There were times when he obviously enjoyed her discomfort and it infuriated me. For me, love isn't about being selfish and controlling; and for that reason, I won't be reading any more of this series.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1810306833783192650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6049660126770203803"><b>Lachlain MacRieve(Lykae) & Emmaline Troy (half Valkyrie/half vampire)</b><br/><br/><i>"Vampires, Valkirie, and Lykae, oh my. The 'fucking monster mash'"</i><br/><br/>Lachlain has just discovered his mate in Paris and he is not sure if he wants her. <br/>You see, his mate is a filthy vampire. <br/>She is one of the revolting creatures that Lachlain has spent all his immortal life chasing and brutally killing without remorse. She is one of the malicious creatures that had him imprisoned and tortured with fire for centuries. <br/><br/>So, this is d</span>
  <span id="freeText6049660126770203803" style="display:none"><b>Lachlain MacRieve(Lykae) &amp; Emmaline Troy (half Valkyrie/half vampire)</b><br /><br /><i>"Vampires, Valkirie, and Lykae, oh my. The 'fucking monster mash'"</i><br /><br />Lachlain has just discovered his mate in Paris and he is not sure if he wants her. <br />You see, his mate is a filthy vampire. <br />She is one of the revolting creatures that Lachlain has spent all his immortal life chasing and brutally killing without remorse. She is one of the malicious creatures that had him imprisoned and tortured with fire for centuries. <br /><br />So, this is definitely a mistake. Fate cannot be that cruel. He cannot be the protector of someone so vile.<br /><br />Emmaline is having a nice, relaxing time in Paris, while she is looking for her father who abandoned her mother before she was born. <br />That night she is sitting on the bench thinking that her trip was in vain and smelling the Paris air, when a brute madman suddenly appears and he starts approaching her. <br /><br /><i>Half-lit by the walk’s torchlights, a towering man turned over café tables, artists’ easels, and book stands selling century-old pornography. Tourists screamed and fled in the wake of destruction.</i><br /><br />Of course Emma runs! And of course it is not really clever to run away from a wolf.<br /><br /><i>He pointed a shaking hand at her. “You,” he growled.</i><br /><br />The setting is magnificent. It felt like Lachlain and Emma are part of a motion picture, something close to the “An American Werewolf in Paris” :)<br /><br />Overall I enjoyed the story, although there were times that I was feeling frustrated with all the misunderstandings:<br />-Emma does not tell Lachlain that she is not exactly a bloodthirsty, sexthirsty vampire. But that she half Valkyrie/half Vampire. And a virgin.<br />- Lachlain does not tell her that she is his destined mate and he treats her like garbage because she is the enemy.<br /><br />As a result there are two distinct parts in the book. The first part in which there are secrets between the two lovers. The second part where they both learn the truth, Lachlain deliciously grovels and Emma embraces her true destiny.<br /><br />I loved the introduction of the Lykae and their castle in the Highlands over the grounds of Kinevane and I loved the Valkyrie family united looking out for each other.</span>

    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300376217?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=adventures">adventures</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=badass-heroine">badass-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=multi-paranormal-species">multi-paranormal-species</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=magical-creatures">magical-creatures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=scotland">scotland</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300376217" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2303938698298092280"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Vampires, Valkyrie, and Lykae, oh my. Or as Regin calls it—the ‘fucking monster mash.’ Hilarity ensued."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I found myself in deep water: first I was confused by the many different creatures, their characterization and history. The story is fast-paced, and Kresley Cole’s wicked humor made me devoted to the series. So far, it was the most comical father-murder I’ve ever read. I was especially delighted at the appearance of Nïx, my most favorite character ever.<br/><br/>I really love this unique an</span>
  <span id="freeText2303938698298092280" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Vampires, Valkyrie, and Lykae, oh my. Or as Regin calls it—the ‘fucking monster mash.’ Hilarity ensued."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I found myself in deep water: first I was confused by the many different creatures, their characterization and history. The story is fast-paced, and Kresley Cole’s wicked humor made me devoted to the series. So far, it was the most comical father-murder I’ve ever read. I was especially delighted at the appearance of Nïx, my most favorite character ever.<br><br>I really love this unique and complex world that Cole created. How she keeps the multiple story lines in hand is really fascinating.<br><br><b>Lachlain and Emma</b> are bonded together by blood, fate and instincts.<br><b>Lachlain</b> is infuriated by the fact that Emma is partly a vampire, but as the story progresses, he suddenly catches himself forgetting about it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391359502i/8377736.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
<i>"He would use this against her,</i> he thought hazily. <i>If his blood on her tongue made her lose control like this, he would force her to drink him until she surrendered everything...<br>Force a vampire to drink him…what was happening to him?"</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Lachlain’s desire for Emma is so strong that it helps him to stay sane after being tortured for 150 years. He is possessive and arrogant, but sometimes has really tender moments:<br><blockquote>
  <i>When he watched her sleeping, he often thought, My heart lies vulnerable outside my chest.</i>
</blockquote><br><b>Emma</b> is a very young immortal. She is only seventy, overprotected by her Valkyrie aunts, delicate, shy and insecure. But she has hidden assets.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391359502i/8377737._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a beast not only in Lachlain, but in Emma as well. Her real strength breaks surface by drinking from Lachlain. His blood, memories, instincts are catalysts for her alteration.<br><br>The gentle, fearful Emma becomes a strong, confident, wily warrior.<br><br>Kinevane<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391359586i/8377751._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Val Hall - Special thanks to <a href="http://virtualneko.com/2008/10/31/happy-nekoween/" rel="nofollow noopener">Stacia Villota </a>for the picture.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380373250i/726786.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/A-Hunger-Like-No-Other" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2303938698298092280" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_945169131" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945169131" />
    <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books"><img alt="Sammy Loves Books" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534119573p2/14227114.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/945169131?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sammy Loves Books" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sammy Loves Books" href="/user/show/14227114-sammy-loves-books">Sammy Loves Books</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=bestiality">bestiality</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=angst-upon-angst">angst-upon-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=do-me-baby">do-me-baby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=he-owns-my-heart">he-owns-my-heart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=werewolves-rule">werewolves-rule</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=stalkerific-alpha">stalkerific-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=vampires-bite">vampires-bite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=virgins-like-sex-too">virgins-like-sex-too</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14227114-sammy-loves-books?shelf=library-book">library-book</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer945169131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10690157772304078325"><blockquote>
  <b>When he watched her sleeping, he often thought,<i> My heart lies vulnerable outside my chest.</i> </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Lachlain MacRieve</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400954459i/9740963.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='alpha' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Lachlain is the King of the Lykae (werewolves) and has spent the last one hundred and fifty years chained under the streets of Paris by an open fire. He burns to death daily, only to regenerate and suffer that cruel death over and over again. His torture at the hands of the vampire horde has no end in site until he smells his mate. But Lachlain has gone insane and his only desire is to</span>
  <span id="freeText10690157772304078325" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>When he watched her sleeping, he often thought,<i> My heart lies vulnerable outside my chest.</i> </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>Lachlain MacRieve</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1400954459i/9740963.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="alpha" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Lachlain is the King of the Lykae (werewolves) and has spent the last one hundred and fifty years chained under the streets of Paris by an open fire. He burns to death daily, only to regenerate and suffer that cruel death over and over again. His torture at the hands of the vampire horde has no end in site until he smells his mate. But Lachlain has gone insane and his only desire is to exact revenge on every living vampire.<br><br>Lachlain goes berserk when he discovers that his mate is a Vampire! How could fate be so cruel to make his one and only mate his mortal enemy? So what if she is weak, frail, small, and docile.<br><br><br><b>Emmaline Troy</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401928470i/9869868.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="emma" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Emma's mother was a Valkyrie and her father was a Vampire. She has been raised by her crazy ass Valkyrie aunts, who are mortal enemies of Vampires. With her genes, Emma should be fierce and strong, but she is afraid of her own shadow. Her motto is to keep her head down, avoid conflict, and if that fails, …RUN!!! In a brief moment of bravery, she travels to Paris alone hoping to discover the identity of her vampire father. <br><br>But Emmaline finds more than just the identity of her father, she finds her mate. And he isn't a nerdy, quiet, gentleman. He's a pissed off Lykae, insane from torture and wild with need of his woman. He's coming for her in full rage and it's a frightening sight!! Emma's instinct is to <b>RUN</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400954459ra/9740965.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="transition" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Never run from one such as me, female. You will no’ get away - and we like it.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was a wonderful story of growth. Emma had grown up coddled, protected, and ashamed of being part vampire. She was literally afraid of her own shadow, and never spoke up for herself. I am usually not a fan of omega types, but I could relate to Emma for some reason. She was a product of her environment, and it took her leaving that cage, to finally become the fierce warrior she was capable of all along. And I loved it!!<br><br><b>Val Hall</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403092062i/10036721.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="val hall" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Lachlain may be a badass werewolf, but his sole purpose was making Emma happy. At lease it is after he gets over her whole vampireism…LOL He hated her for the first half of the book, even though he wanted to bone her brains out. Oh, the angst!! Plus, I'm a sucker for a tortured hero. His attempts at seduction had me panting and ready, but Emma was not as easy as I am. Needless to say, I was BEYOND ready for these two to "seal the deal" by the time it happened.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Now, undress for me and let me see what’s mine.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400856039ra/9728511.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="passion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I am loving this series so far and can't wait to read the next installment. I love this world of Vampires, Werewolves, Valkyrie, and Witches…It's a Paranormal romance fan's dream come true.<br><br><br><b>My Immortals After Dark Reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945149690" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945169131" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/949584205" rel="nofollow noopener">No Rest for the Wicked</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172183" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172557" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs at Night's Edge</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172787" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dark Desires After Dusk</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/994211489" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of a Demon King</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945174408" rel="nofollow noopener">Untouchable</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945178167" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180198" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180215" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreams of a Dark Warrior</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1289048120" rel="nofollow noopener">Lothaire</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400296552" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Skye</a></b></span>

<div id="review_49479176" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/49479176" />
    <a title="LMM" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1533889-lmm"><img alt="LMM" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393087075p2/1533889.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/49479176?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="LMM" class="user" itemprop="url" name="LMM" href="/user/show/1533889-lmm">LMM</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Hardcore Romance Junkies, Paranormal Romace</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to LMM by: </span>
      Book club
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1533889-lmm?shelf=overrated">overrated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1533889-lmm?shelf=paranormal-pnr">paranormal-pnr</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer49479176" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13103958372822434557">Wow I thought this was pretty bad. I know I am in the minority but I found the plot was really thin. I also felt all the characters were incredibly "thick"(except Bove) esp. Emma & her family. IMO, There are far better paranormal "romance" books. I just didn't connect w/the characters at all nor the author's justifications for their actions.<br/><br/>Basically the book followed the Romance formula authors are forced to follow by their publishers to a T:<br/><br/>Sexually experienced to the hilt, hung like a horse A</span>
  <span id="freeText13103958372822434557" style="display:none">Wow I thought this was pretty bad. I know I am in the minority but I found the plot was really thin. I also felt all the characters were incredibly "thick"(except Bove) esp. Emma &amp; her family. IMO, There are far better paranormal "romance" books. I just didn't connect w/the characters at all nor the author's justifications for their actions.<br /><br />Basically the book followed the Romance formula authors are forced to follow by their publishers to a T:<br /><br />Sexually experienced to the hilt, hung like a horse Alpha Male meets his true Virginal mate (or vice versa - apparently, these men are just as surprised at I am they these woman are still virgins. <br /><br />One of them is reluctant &amp; fights the attraction by usually believing something not true about the person, about 50% through the book is when something sexual happens - so they either have sex for the 1st time OR something big sexually happens but they don't have sex.<br /><br />If they don't have sex @ the 50% mark - more misunderstanding high-jinks ensue until about 70-79% When the deed is actually done.<br /><br />At 80% the big bad starts to be dealt with. By 90% is being confronted &amp; by 95-100% the author ties up the happy ending.<br /> <br />In this book - The main character is an insecure, whiny, spoiled, cruel, shrew. The man is very Alpha &amp; grunts his speech 1/2 the time but he is a hell of a lot better than her &amp; her insane family. The plot is lame &amp; the the formula is dog tired.<br /><br />The worst part is that actually, the man from the beginning tries to find out more about the MC &amp; explain himself but she won't hear it. The author's excuse? "She's secretive" &amp; "she wants to protect her family." From what I don't know b'c they happen to be lethal - it's just all a series of excessively dumb assumptions.<br /><br />I suppose I would say this is really technically "paranormal romance" &amp; that's that.<br /><br />I don't recommend unless the person is a hardcore romance junkie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13103958372822434557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1150443860227158411"><br/>I am going to keep this short and sweet because I am eager to get back to 'KC-land'!!<br/><br/>Maybe because I've been craving something different or maybe because Kresley Cole has such excellent way with words but I love being lost in this magical world she created so masterfully and don't want to find my way out any time soon!   <span id="freeText1150443860227158411" style="display:none"><br>I am going to keep this short and sweet because I am eager to get back to 'KC-land'!!<br><br>Maybe because I've been craving something different or maybe because Kresley Cole has such excellent way with words but I love being lost in this magical world she created so masterfully and don't want to find my way out any time soon! The way this author tells stories ... GAH! I can't even ... Her books are PURE ENTERTAINMENT! They are a perfect mix of sass, macho, sexy and humor! They always leave me smiling like a lunatic during and after. At this point [in this series especially!] I don't even care WHOSE book it is - I just want to keep on reading! I love that she makes me love equally ALL of her characters who can't be any more different from one another. THAT, my friends, is talent! <br><br>If you haven't yet experienced the magic of Kresley Cole's writing, do it NOW! She has several genres/series to choose from and ALL of those are top notch, in my opinion! <br><br>Cheers!<br><br><a href="http://amzn.to/2bhRv28" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_181697202" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/181697202" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/181697202?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen">Kristen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6473141-a-hunger-like-no-other">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Kristen by: </span>
      Karla
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=humorous">humorous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=lots-of-bickering">lots-of-bickering</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5477946-kristen?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181697202" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7487884373810211200"><b>3 1/2 to 4 stars</b><br/><br/>Overall I really enjoyed reading <i>A Hunger Like No Other</i>, the first full-length book in the Immortals After Dark series by Kresley Cole. <br/><br/>I'm truly in awe of Ms. Cole's ability to create a complex and intriguing paranormal world full of Vampires, Lykaes (werewolves), Valkyries, Demons, Witches, Feys, Ghouls, and the list goes on and on. Although this paranormal world is complex, Ms. Cole has the ability to easily explain her intricate world to the reader, making this book an enjoya</span>
  <span id="freeText7487884373810211200" style="display:none"><b>3 1/2 to 4 stars</b><br /><br />Overall I really enjoyed reading <i>A Hunger Like No Other</i>, the first full-length book in the Immortals After Dark series by Kresley Cole. <br /><br />I'm truly in awe of Ms. Cole's ability to create a complex and intriguing paranormal world full of Vampires, Lykaes (werewolves), Valkyries, Demons, Witches, Feys, Ghouls, and the list goes on and on. Although this paranormal world is complex, Ms. Cole has the ability to easily explain her intricate world to the reader, making this book an enjoyable read. <br /><br />As much as I liked this action packed, intriguing, humorous, and highly sensual story filled with mostly likable characters, there were a few plot inconsistencies that bothered me. For instance, the Horde captures, imprisons, and tortures Lachlain, the hero, only to have him eventually escape decades later, then never bother to pursue him or even give him an afterthought. That does not make sense! Then we have the heroine, Emma, whom everyone considers meek, timid, and in constant need of protection. Yet, her Valkyrie coven allows her to travel alone and unprotected to Paris in search of information about her deceased mother and her unknown vampire father, though vampires are the Valkyries' known enemy.  <br /><br />I will also admit to being a little annoyed with the slow developing progress of the relationship between the hero and heroine and their constant bickering; however, I also understand that the author used their relationship as a tool to flesh out her world in this first full-lenght book of the series. Knowing that allowed me to get past my annoyance and to enjoy their relationship for what it was. <br /><br />A special thanks to the author for include in the back of her book an easy to understand glossary titled From the Book of Lore, which made it relatively easy for the reader to comprehend her world.  <br /><br /><i>A Hunger Like No Other</i> was  a fun, engaging and very sexy read. I very much look forward to reading this series.  <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7487884373810211200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_45256223" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/45256223" />
    <a title="Dina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1918270-dina"><img alt="Dina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460302951p2/1918270.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/45256223?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dina" href="/user/show/1918270-dina">Dina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=series-immortals-after-dark">series-immortals-after-dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1918270-dina?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer45256223" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3479939035986088648">This is the first full-length story in the <b>Immortals After Dark</b> series, following the novella <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_' title='The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a> that introduced the <i>Lore</i>, the mythical strata created by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole' title='Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kresley Cole</a> "where those sentient creatures that are not human live". You don’t have to read that short story to understand <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_' title='A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a>, but I did and I think it helps to get a better grasp of the overall scenario as some events in the two stories take place at the same time.<br/><br/>Lachlain MacRieve is the Lykae King</span>
  <span id="freeText3479939035986088648" style="display:none">This is the first full-length story in the <b>Immortals After Dark</b> series, following the novella <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a> that introduced the <i>Lore</i>, the mythical strata created by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a> "where those sentient creatures that are not human live". You don’t have to read that short story to understand <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/14384.A_Hunger_Like_No_Other__Immortals_After_Dark___2_" title="A Hunger Like No Other (Immortals After Dark, #2) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a>, but I did and I think it helps to get a better grasp of the overall scenario as some events in the two stories take place at the same time.<br /><br />Lachlain MacRieve is the Lykae King, a 1,200-year-old werewolf who’s been searching for his mate for a long, long time. For the past 150 years, he’s been imprisoned in the catacombs beneath Paris, where he’s been tortured by the Vampire Horde and subjected to die from the fires of hell only to be resurrected by his immortality - over and over again. The only thing that keeps him alive and somewhat sane is the thought of finding his mate, so when he unexpectedly <i>scents</i> her nearby one night, he finds the strength to break free from the bonds that keep him captive. When he finally escapes the catacombs and finds his way to the surface, then into a darkened alley, his mate is gone. He’s not defeated, though, because once a Lykae scents his mate, she’s his forever – and he will find her again… However, Lachlain has the shock of his life when he catches up with her one week later and discovers she’s, gasp!, a vampire. No, this cannot be! Lykaes and vampires are mortal enemies, so why would fate give him a vampire as a mate?<br /><br />Emmaline “Emma” Troy is actually half vampire and half Valkyrie. Her mother Helen (of Troy?) was a Valkyrie who died when Emma was still a baby. As for her father, all Emma knows is that he is/was a vampire. Determined to finally find out his identity, Emma’s left the Valkyrie coven in New Orleans for the first time in her 70 years – wow, she’s almost a newborn compared to Lachlain! – and flies to Paris, where her parents are believed to have met and lived together for a while. Imagine her surprise when, one night, she’s kidnapped by a strange non-human male who seems to be a bit "deranged", to say the least.<br /><br />Lachlain is torn between lust and disgust. His "beast" wants to claim Emma as his mate, but he’s having a hard time reconciling the fact that she’s a vampire. He ends up "convincing" her to travel with him to his home in Scotland, with the promise that he’ll let her go when they get there. He’s lying through his teeth, of course, as he has no intention of letting her go – ever! He’s only buying time, before she accepts her position as his mate. But there are people after her – not only her Valkyrie foster mother and aunts, but some bad vampires too – and Lachlain has to fight all of them to keep Emma safe. Not an easy task, when he has to woo her and convince her she belongs with him at the same time.<br /><br />When I read the Prologue, I thought Lachlain would end up being one of my favorite heroes. I was sure he would be a dark, brooding and intense hero – come on, he severed one of his leg to free it from its bonds to get to his mate! – but that was not to be. He had a brief bout of "insanity" in the beginning, which was completely expected considering his 150-year imprisonment, but he recovered from it quite easily and I found it too unbelievable. Strangely enough, I wasn’t put off by his lying to Emma. I’m usually not a fan of deceitful heroes, but I was OK with Lachlain’s lying because it was consistent with his initial "madness". He kept lying later, when he was "sane" again, but that was another story...<br /><br />As for Emma, she got on my nerves. She started out as a wuss – by her own words – and ended up as a strong and independent vampire/Valkyrie – kudos to her! – but the journey in between was uneven. I guess she was supposed to be funny and witty, but I found myself wanting to shake some sense into her a couple of times. Some of her conversations with her crazy Valkyrie aunts were hilarious, but I got tired of their antics after a while. There’s a time to joke around, and there’s a time to get down to business. JMHO.<br /><br />I could have "ignored" Lachlan’s and Emma’s shortcomings if the plot had been engaging enough but, alas, that wasn’t the case. Some jarring inconsistencies kept pestering me while I was reading this book, and I just couldn’t get over them. A) Lachlain’s escape from the catacombs wasn’t as difficult as it should have been. I mean, not a single guard intercepted his way! B) Why did Lachlain waited 150 years to escape? Don’t tell me that he only felt compelled to do it when he scented Emma, because I can’t believe he didn’t find ending his torture as soon as possible compelling enough. C) Why didn’t the Vampire Horde go after Lachlain when he escaped? He couldn’t be that "insignificant", could he? D) Why did Demestriu, the Vampire King, … Okay, I’ll stop ranting now because I’m about to enter into spoiler territory.<br /><br />All things considered, this was a fun read but, as it happened with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark___1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark, #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a>, I wasn’t wowed by the story. I’m feeling kind of weird here, because many readers love this series and I just don’t get it. I do love the idea of having all kinds of non-human beings living together – mostly at war but some in peace – in the same universe, the <i>Lore</i>, but that’s all. Ms. Cole’s writing was humorous and easy to read, the love scenes were hot and the story was fast paced and entertaining despite its inconsistencies, but I’m still unsure about this series. Does it get better? Should I give the next book a try? Decisions, decisions…<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3479939035986088648" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1101621579" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1101621579" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1101621579?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/12908993-a-hunger-like-no-other">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Carmel (Rabid Reads) by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/2806016-melanie">Melanie</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2014">audio-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1101621579" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13727200985501091066"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/03/audiobook-review-a-hunger-like-no-other-by-kresley-cole.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>After a lot of arm twisting by fellow readers, getting hooked on Cole’s writing via THE ARCANA CHRONILES, and listening to a sample of Robert Petkoff’s orgasm worthy narration; I finally caved and committed myself to yet another series addiction. I enjoy Paranormal Romance, although somewhat sparingly because action is my one-and-only true love. Ok, that’s not entirely accurate, werewolves are but the two go hand-in-hand, and this audiobook has both AND toe curling hooks</span>
  <span id="freeText13727200985501091066" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/03/audiobook-review-a-hunger-like-no-other-by-kresley-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />After a lot of arm twisting by fellow readers, getting hooked on Cole’s writing via THE ARCANA CHRONILES, and listening to a sample of Robert Petkoff’s orgasm worthy narration; I finally caved and committed myself to yet another series addiction. I enjoy Paranormal Romance, although somewhat sparingly because action is my one-and-only true love. Ok, that’s not entirely accurate, werewolves are but the two go hand-in-hand, and this audiobook has both AND toe curling hooks ups, so really A HUNGER LIKE NO OTHER was win / win / WIN!<br /><br />You know an author is truly adept when she manages to take two elements that rank fairly low on your list of awesome, and makes you love them. I strongly dislike immortal virgin heroines because honestly, how can one live for centuries and NEVER get it on? Granted, Emmaline hasn’t hit the 100 year mark, however Cole spun her innocence in such a way that even I was completely sold. And secondly, Valkyries have become more common in Paranormal than vampires and the female protagonist just so happens to be a mix of the two, and yet I couldn’t have cared less because her character was so well developed that I saw her as a person rather than just the sum on her preternatural parts.<br /><br />Lachlain was barbaric, offensive, and presumptuous; he whisked unwitting little Emma away to his Scottish castle, tried to force himself on her, and strong-arm her into becoming his werewolf queen—I loved it! The chemistry between them was downright savage. MacRieve hates himself for being unable to resist his mortal enemy, Troy is repulsed by his Lykae nature, and yet they are inexplicably drawn to each other like moths to a flame. Their relationship and the mind blowing romp that followed were indeed show stoppers, however the praiseworthy world-building surrounding the Lore wasn’t too far behind. The plot wasn’t exactly cutting-edge, but enough secondary threads were brought in to keep IMMORTALS AFTER DARK going for a good long while.<br /><br />As much as I enjoy Cole’s writing style, it was Robert Petkoff’s come-hither brogue that made thirteen+ IAD installments seem like a walk in the park. Yes, the number of pages involved is intimidating, but when you convert them into hours upon hours of listening ecstasy, the only conceivable answer becomes “Where do I sign-up?” His female voices were surprisingly genuine, and there’s no denying the sex appeal of his Scottish accents. Lachlain as a character was… abrasive, however Petkoff’s rendition made him ridiculously irresistible. Now I finally understand why all of my reviewer peers are fawning over this narrator; he truly is in a league all of his own.<br /><br />A HUNGER LIKE NO OTHER made me want to give real life the middle finger, and get drunk on IAD until I overdosed. <b>~4.5 stars</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13727200985501091066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
